===== ITEM 0 =====
LABEL: CLONE

PAGE 1:
- **Main Action:** View and manage events for August 17, 2019, in Room 5 of Area 2.
- **Secondary Actions:** Navigate to previous or next days, weeks, or months; switch between internal and external views.
- **Goal:** Efficiently organize and access event details for the specified date.

###

PAGE 2:
- **Main Action:** Access detailed information about events scheduled on August 17, 2019.
- **Secondary Actions:** Switch between different views (external/internal) and navigate through various dates and time slots.
- **Goal:** Ensure all relevant parties can easily find and manage the day's schedule.
